We are continuing the discussion about MenuApp Client Home Screen UX. Here was your previous analysis (summarized key points):

YOUR PREVIOUS POSITION (Codex Round 1):
- Hierarchy: Header > Status strip > Mode tabs > Verify block > Search > Category chips > Menu > Sticky cart > Help FAB
- Search field above categories as high-value element
- You are here status strip as separate block
- First-time coach mark / helper
- Mode tabs always visible
- Hall verification BEFORE menu (inline, before search)
- Branding compact, speed to menu first
- Anti-patterns: popups, mandatory login, long about us, too many CTAs

MY PERSPECTIVE (Claude/CC) -- based on deep project context:

1. SEARCH IS LOW VALUE HERE. Unlike Wolt/Yandex with 1000s of items, a single restaurant has 20-60 dishes across 5-10 categories. Category chips are enough for discovery. Search adds visual noise on an already complex screen (2442 lines, 22 components). Search should be OPTIONAL -- hidden behind a magnifying glass icon, not a visible field.

2. SEPARATE STATUS STRIP IS UNNECESSARY. Table 22 Dine-in can be embedded in the header itself. Every extra visual block pushes real content (menu items) down. On mobile, pixels above the fold are precious.

3. FIRST-TIME COACH MARKS ARE OVER-ENGINEERING. QR ordering is a browse-tap-cart flow -- self-explanatory. Guests understand see food then tap then cart without instruction. Adding dismissible helpers adds complexity (state management, localStorage, render logic) for minimal gain. The flow should be intuitive by design, not explained by overlay.

In reality, hall logic is in `const processHallOrder = async (guestToUse, validatedSession) => {...}` at line 3671, called from `handleSubmitOrder` at line 4039. The delivery block IS inline in `handleSubmitOrder` (line 4045â€“4210). The prompt's refactoring instructions assume a flat code structure â€” CC may misidentify where to apply changes. PROMPT FIX: Explicitly name the two functions: "Refactor `processHallOrder` (line 3671) for hall mode" and "Refactor the inline delivery/takeaway block in `handleSubmitOrder` (line 4045) for non-hall mode."

3. **[CRITICAL] `order_number` / `getNextOrderNumber` not addressed for N orders.** Hall mode calls `getNextOrderNumber(partner, 'hall')` at line 3709, which returns ONE `orderNumber` and ONE `updatedCounters` object. With N orders, each order needs its own unique `order_number`, requiring N calls to `getNextOrderNumber`. The prompt's code snippet uses `...orderData` which would give ALL N orders the SAME `order_number`. This will cause order number collisions visible to staff. PROMPT FIX: Add explicit instruction: "Call `getNextOrderNumber(partner, orderType)` inside the loop for each order â€” each split order must have a unique `order_number`. Accumulate all `updatedCounters` and apply the final counter state once after the loop."

4. **[CRITICAL] `updatedCounters` must be recalculated for N orders.** `getNextOrderNumber` increments the partner's internal counter. With N orders, calling it N times in the loop means each call must see the incremented state from the previous call. The prompt doesn't mention this at all. If `getNextOrderNumber` reads from `partner` object (stale closure), all N orders get the same number. PROMPT FIX: Add instruction to pass accumulated counter state to each successive `getNextOrderNumber` call, or explain how the function handles sequential calls.

5. **[CRITICAL] Rollback deletes Orders but doesn't rollback OrderItems.** The rollback code in the prompt deletes Orders (`Order.delete(o.id)`), but OrderItems were already created in the same loop iteration. If `OrderItem.create` at iteration 3 fails, iterations 1 and 2 have both Orders AND OrderItems. Deleting the Order may not cascade-delete OrderItems (depends on B44 behavior). PROMPT FIX: Either (a) confirm B44 cascade-deletes OrderItems when Order is deleted, or (b) add explicit `OrderItem.delete` in rollback, or (c) restructure: create all Orders first, then all OrderItems.

6. **[MEDIUM] `splitType` not available in delivery/takeaway branch.** The prompt acknowledges this ("use `'single'` as fallback") but the code snippet references `splitType ?? 'single'` in the `OrderItem.create` call. In the delivery branch (line 4115â€“4122), the existing code does NOT include `split_type` at all. Adding it as `'single'` is harmless but the prompt should be explicit about whether to add this field to the delivery branch items or omit it to match existing behavior. PROMPT FIX: Clarify: "In the delivery/takeaway branch, do NOT add `split_type` to OrderItem (matching current behavior which omits it)."

7. **[MEDIUM] `setSessionOrders` optimistic update must handle N orders, not 1.** The prompt says "add ALL N created orders" but doesn't show the code. Current code (line 3817â€“3820) does dedup check `prev.some(o => String(o.id) === String(order.id))`. With N orders, this needs to add all N and dedup each. The implementer might not get this right without a code snippet. PROMPT FIX: Add explicit code snippet for the N-order optimistic update: `setSessionOrders(prev => { const newOrders = createdOrders.filter(co => !prev.some(o => String(o.id) === String(co.id))).map(co => ({...co, guest: guestToUse?.id, _optimisticAt: Date.now()})); return [...newOrders, ...prev]; });`

8. **[MEDIUM] `showConfirmation` receives `publicToken: order.public_token` â€” but with N orders, which token?** The prompt says "use `createdOrders[0].public_token`" which is correct, but `showConfirmation` also receives `items: confirmedItems` and `totalAmount: confirmedTotal`. The `totalAmount` should remain `finalTotal` (the combined total, not one order's total). The prompt doesn't clarify this. PROMPT FIX: Add explicit instruction: "Pass `totalAmount: finalTotal` (pre-existing variable, the full cart total) to `showConfirmation` â€” NOT the per-item total."

# Codex Reviewer Findings â€” ÐŸÐ¡Ð¡Ðš Prompt Quality Review
Chain: publicmenu-260407-104609-7148

## Issues Found
1. [CRITICAL] Entity API is internally inconsistent â€” The prompt tells the implementer to grep for `Order.create(orderData)` / `OrderItem.bulkCreate`, but the replacement snippet switches to `base44.entities.Order.create(...)` / `base44.entities.OrderItem.create(...)`. If `base44` is not the current in-scope API in `x.jsx`, a literal implementation will fail or mix patterns inside one handler. PROMPT FIX: say "keep the existing entity access pattern already used in `x.jsx`; replace only the 1-order + bulkCreate flow with a loop." Remove hard-coded `base44.entities.*` unless confirmed by the current file.
2. [CRITICAL] "One order per cart item" does not guarantee per-dish control â€” The business goal is per-dish fulfillment, but the prompt loops over `cart` entries and preserves `quantity: item.quantity`. If a cart line has quantity 2 or 3 of the same dish, this still creates one order containing multiple units, so SOM may still advance multiple physical dishes together. PROMPT FIX: explicitly define the required behavior for `quantity > 1`. Either explode line items into unit orders (`quantity: 1` repeated N times) or change the acceptance criteria to say control is per cart line, not per dish.
3. [CRITICAL] Shared charges and item metadata are under-specified â€” `total_amount: itemTotal` is computed only from `price * quantity - discount`. That ignores delivery fees, service fees, packaging, tips, and similar shared charges. The sample `OrderItem.create(...)` also only includes a small field subset and may drop modifiers, add-ons, notes, or variant data carried by the current `bulkCreate` mapping. PROMPT FIX: instruct the implementer to preserve every existing `Order` and `OrderItem` field from the current code, and explicitly define how any non-item charges are allocated in delivery/takeaway mode.
4. [CRITICAL] Rollback is not fully defined and assumes cascade behavior â€” The prompt says to delete created orders on failure, but does not say whether deleting an `Order` automatically deletes its `OrderItem`. It also does not define what happens if failure occurs after the loop during loyalty attach, partner counter update, confirmation setup, or cart clear. That can leave partial data or inconsistent side effects. PROMPT FIX: define the atomic boundary. State whether `Order.delete` cascades to `OrderItem`; if not, delete created items explicitly. Also specify whether post-loop failures must trigger rollback of orders/items and how loyalty/counter side effects are compensated.
5. [MEDIUM] `splitType ?? 'single'` is not a safe fallback if `splitType` is undeclared â€” The prompt later admits `splitType` may not be available in one branch, but the sample code still references it directly. In JavaScript, `splitType ?? 'single'` throws if `splitType` was never declared. PROMPT FIX: replace the sample with a safe rule such as "preserve the current branch's field mapping; if no `splitType` variable exists there, use the literal `'single'`."
6. [MEDIUM] Scope lock conflicts with required changes â€” The prompt says "modify ONLY the two order-creation blocks" and "do NOT change any state," but later requires changing `showConfirmation(...)`, `setSessionOrders`, and `setSessionItems`. Those are likely adjacent but not necessarily inside the narrow create blocks. PROMPT FIX: redefine scope as "changes are limited to `handleSubmitOrder` logic in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`, including post-submit optimistic updates and confirmation token wiring."
7. [MEDIUM] Confirmation token strategy is ambiguous â€” The prompt requires unique `public_token` per split order but then says to use only `createdOrders[0].public_token` for confirmation. If confirmation or later reloads fetch by `public_token`, only one order may be recoverable after refresh, even if optimistic state initially looks correct. PROMPT FIX: state exactly how confirmation/cart reload should resolve the full split submission after a hard refresh, and whether grouping is by guest, session, table, or another stable key.
8. [MEDIUM] Discount rules are incomplete for zero/free/full-discount edge cases â€” The sample math divides by `cartSubtotal` and assumes it is positive. It also does not say how to clamp negative `itemTotal` values when discounts equal or exceed subtotal, or how to handle free items mixed with paid items. PROMPT FIX: add explicit rules for `cartSubtotal <= 0`, free items, full-cart discounts, and negative-total prevention. Define rounding and clamping behavior unambiguously.
9. [MEDIUM] Side-effect semantics are not defined for partner counters and loyalty â€” "Call `Partner.update(updatedCounters)` once, not N times" and "attach loyalty to `createdOrders[0]` only" may be correct, but the prompt never states whether those systems are meant to count cart submissions or actual orders. After the split, analytics, daily counters, rewards, refunds, and staff metrics may drift. PROMPT FIX: specify the intended business semantics for counters and loyalty after splitting, including whether counts should increment by 1 submission or by N persisted orders.
10. [MEDIUM] Verification is too UI-heavy and does not prove persisted correctness â€” Most checks are manual UI checks and can pass from optimistic state even if persisted orders are wrong. There is no explicit check for hard refresh, duplicate-submit behavior with slower sequential creates, orphan records after rollback, or branch-specific shared fields (`guest`, `table`, `table_session`, address) surviving on every created order. PROMPT FIX: add verification for hard refresh/reload, double-tap/submit-lock behavior, rollback cleanup, and persistence of shared fields in both hall and delivery/takeaway branches.
11. [LOW] Search guidance is brittle for the stated environment â€” The prompt uses `grep -n ...` commands and fixed approximate line numbers. In a Windows/PowerShell workflow, `grep` may not exist, and stale line offsets encourage brittle navigation. PROMPT FIX: use shell-neutral guidance or `rg` examples, and label line numbers as approximate hints only, not expected locations.

Stale requests therefore remain active indefinitely. FIX: add a Help-scoped `useEffect` that runs on `timerTick`, filters `activeRequests` by `Date.now() - sentAt > 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000`, and resolves each stale row through local `handleResolve(type, otherId)` without introducing a new polling interval or backend call.

function lightenColor(hex, amount) {
  const num = parseInt(hex.replace('#', ''), 16);
  const r = Math.min(255, (num >> 16) + Math.round((255 - (num >> 16)) * amount));
  const g = Math.min(255, ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF) + Math.round((255 - ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF)) * amount));
  const b = Math.min(255, (num & 0x0000FF) + Math.round((255 - (num & 0x0000FF)) * amount));
  return `#${(r << 16 | g << 8 | b).toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`;
}

A C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/review_2026-04-13.md
## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt

### Scope
This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.

I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`

### Findings

- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".

- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.

- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
  - keep the parent API untouched
  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.

- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.

- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.

- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.

- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
  - an optional bell action
  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
  - a second line for order count + sum
  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.

- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
  - served-only / history-only state
  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
  - other-guests/table-total behavior
  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.

### Summary
- Total findings: 7
- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
- Most important prompt changes:
  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule

### Practical Recommendation
Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
- a status mapping table
- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
- transition rules for auto-collapse
- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

codex
The current `CartView.jsx` looks like it’s stored with null bytes/UTF-16, which makes normal grep slower. I have enough evidence for the findings themselves, and I’m checking just the smallest slices I need for supporting references.

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps
