+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt

### Scope
This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.

I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`

### Findings

- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "ÐŸÐ¾Ð´Ð°Ð½Ð¾/Ð—Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·Ð°Ð½Ð¾" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".

- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.

- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "ÐÐ¾Ð²Ñ‹Ð¹ Ð·Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
  - keep the parent API untouched

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
+  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
+  - keep the parent API untouched
+  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
+  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
+  - an optional bell action
+  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
+  - a second line for order count + sum
+  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
+  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only / history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
+  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 7
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

D C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/review_2026-04-13.md
## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt

### Scope
This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.

I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`

### Findings

- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx` around the `statusBuckets` `useMemo`, while guest-facing labels are normalized separately in `getSafeStatus()` earlier in the file. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "Подано/Заказано" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include an explicit mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by `getSafeStatus().label`".

- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. In `CartView.jsx:623-647`, the UI can only infer `saving` vs "has draft/has review" from current props. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.

- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx` (the file only keeps the dead prop plumbing and a removal comment near the "Новый заказ" section), but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772` and accepted in `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32-33`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to:
  - delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`
  - keep the parent API untouched
  - or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too
  That is a safety issue because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.

- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`837-843`), each bucket subtotal (`885-907`, `960-983`), and the "Новый заказ" subtotal (`1021-1028`). If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the "Новый заказ" section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove table for every money surface.

- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.

- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows hide `×1` and show `×N` only when `totalQty > 1` in `renderBucketOrders`, cart rows show the secondary `price × qty` line only when `item.quantity > 1` in the "Новый заказ" section, while table-orders rows still print `× {item.quantity}` unconditionally in the "Заказы стола" section. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.

- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains:
  - an optional bell action
  - inline guest-name edit mode with two 44px actions
  - a second line for order count + sum
  - a close chevron guarded by `isSubmitting`
  These all live in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.

- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
  - served-only / history-only state
  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
  - other-guests/table-total behavior
  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm`, `splitType`, `myBill`
  If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural CartView rewrite.

### Summary
- Total findings: 7
- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 3
- Most important prompt changes:
  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView`-only or also requires `x.jsx`
  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule

### Practical Recommendation
Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
- a status mapping table
- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, bucket subtotal, cart subtotal, and footer money
- transition rules for auto-collapse
- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

A C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/review_2026-04-13.md
## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt

### Scope
This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.

I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`

### Findings

- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".

- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.

- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.

- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.

- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.

- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.

- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.

- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
  - served-only/history-only state
  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
  - other-guests/table-total behavior
  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.

### Summary
- Total findings: 8
- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
- Most important prompt changes:
  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule

### Practical Recommendation
Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
- a status mapping table
- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
- transition rules for auto-collapse
- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

codex
The saved artifacts are updated. I’m doing one quick pass on the report file and then I’ll close with the findings and file links.

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

codex
**Findings**

- [P1] Fix 1 is under-specified. The prompt says “collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups,” but the current component still groups by raw `order.status` in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:402) and still initializes five expand buckets in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:93). If the prompt does not explicitly map raw statuses like `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new`, the implementation can collapse the wrong buckets.

- [P1] Fix 3 is incomplete unless the prompt widens scope beyond `CartView.jsx`. The save flow lives in [x.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297), and today it only exposes boolean `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]`. There is no defined “A2” state contract in the parent. A prompt that asks for “submit feedback state A2” without defining where that state comes from is likely to produce invalid snippets or missing variables.

- [P1] Fix 5 is a scope/safety risk. The split UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but dead prop plumbing still exists in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32) and is still passed from [x.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771). “Remove split-type” is ambiguous unless the prompt explicitly says whether cleanup is `CartView.jsx` only or also includes `x.jsx`. Otherwise the implementer may touch files the prompt did not intend.

- [P1] Fix 2 is ambiguous. “Money only in header” is not precise enough because money currently appears in multiple places: header sum in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:417), table total card in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:842), status-group subtotals, and new-order subtotal. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for each money surface.

- [P2] Fix 4 needs transition semantics. The current auto-collapse effect only reacts to the `cart.length > 0` transition in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:96). The prompt should state whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether sections should reopen when the cart becomes empty again.

- [P2] Fix 6 is ambiguous across render paths. Quantity is not rendered in one place only; grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-order rows use different rules. “Fix qty display” needs to name every affected surface, or the implementer will likely patch one path and miss the others.

- [P2] Fix 7 is too subjective as written. The header currently includes optional call-waiter action, guest-name edit mode, count/sum line, and an `isSubmitting`-guarded close action in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:673). “Compact header” should define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and disabled-close state on mobile.

- [P2] Post-fix checks are too weak unless they verify both UI and contract cleanup. The prompt should require checks for empty vs non-empty cart, served-only state, rating save/fail/retry flow, narrow mobile header layout, and parent/child prop alignment between `x.jsx` and `CartView.jsx`. It should also explicitly check for leftover dead state like `showRewardEmailForm` in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:114).

No P0 issue is evident from the available material, but the biggest prompt-design problem is scope ambiguity: several fixes read as `CartView.jsx`-only, while at least one of them clearly depends on `x.jsx`.

I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked repo artifacts or git metadata in this workspace, so this review is based on the current [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx), [x.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx), and your 7-fix summary.

+## Prompt Design Review: CartView Redesign Prompt
+
+### Scope
+This is a review of the implementation prompt design, not a code review of the final UI.
+
+I could not retrieve the raw branch task body from tracked files or git metadata in this workspace. The findings below are based on:
+- the current 1163-line `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`
+- the upstream contract in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx`
+- the 7-fix summary provided in the request
+- earlier prompt-review artifacts already saved for `PublicMenu`
+
+### Findings
+
+- [P1] Fix 1 (`collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups`) is under-specified unless the prompt names the raw status mapping and the grouping source. The current file still builds `statusBuckets` from raw `order.status` values in `CartView.jsx:402`, while the expanded-state shape still assumes five buckets in `CartView.jsx:93-99`. A prompt that talks only in UI labels like "served/ordered" or "2 groups" without explicitly mapping `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new` is likely to produce the wrong filters. The prompt should include a mapping table and say "group by raw `order.status`, not by display labels".
+
+- [P1] Fix 3 (`submit feedback state A2`) cannot be implemented in `CartView.jsx` alone unless the prompt explicitly widens scope to `x.jsx` and defines the new state contract. The actual rating mutation lives in `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297-3330`, where `handleRateDish` only toggles `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]` between `true` and `false`, rolls back `draftRatings` on failure, and never exposes any `A2` or richer tri-state submit object. `CartView.jsx` only receives those props from the parent. If the prompt names a new `A2` state without defining where it comes from, the snippet is incomplete or uses variables that do not exist.
+
+- [P1] Fix 5 (`remove split-type`) is stale against the current file shape and creates scope risk. The split-order UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but `splitType` and `setSplitType` are still accepted in `CartView.jsx:32-33` and still passed from `pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771-4772`. A prompt that simply says "remove split-type" does not tell the implementer whether to delete only dead props from `CartView.jsx`, keep the parent API untouched, or remove the parent prop plumbing in `x.jsx` too. That is a safety risk because it invites unintended file changes outside the target component.
+
+- [P1] Fix 2 (`money only in header`) is ambiguous because money is currently rendered in several different semantic places, not one. The current component shows money in the header order sum (`CartView.jsx:417`, rendered at `713-720`), the table-total card (`CartView.jsx:842`), each status-group subtotal, and the new-order subtotal. If the prompt only says "money only in header", it does not tell the implementer whether the table-total card survives, whether the cart subtotal still belongs in the new-order section, or whether other-guests/table amounts are exempt. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for every money surface.
+
+- [P2] Fix 4 (`auto-collapse logic`) needs transition semantics, not just a desired end state. The current effect collapses sections only on the boolean transition to `cart.length > 0` in `CartView.jsx:96-110`. The prompt should say whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether groups should reopen automatically when the cart goes back to empty. Without that, a naive implementation will keep fighting user interaction and repeatedly collapse sections after every quantity change.
+
+- [P2] Fix 6 (`qty display`) is ambiguous because quantity appears in multiple render paths with different rules today. Grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-orders rows do not share one formatting rule. The prompt needs to say exactly which surfaces change; otherwise the implementer will almost certainly patch one path and miss the others.
+
+- [P2] Fix 7 (`compact header`) is incomplete unless the prompt defines the mobile and interaction edge cases. The current header contains an optional bell action, inline guest-name edit mode, a second line for order count plus sum, and a close action guarded by `isSubmitting` in `CartView.jsx:673-734`. A prompt that only says "make header compact" but does not define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and in-flight submit close-lock leaves too much room for subjective edits and regression.
+
+- [P2] Post-fix checks are not sufficient unless they verify both UI states and the parent contract. For this redesign, a good verification block should explicitly cover:
+  - cart empty vs cart non-empty
+  - served-only/history-only state
+  - rating save, fail, and re-entry flows
+  - header layout with long names on narrow mobile width
+  - other-guests/table-total behavior
+  - `x.jsx` still matching the final `CartView` prop list
+  - no leftover dead state/props such as `showRewardEmailForm` (`CartView.jsx:114`), `splitType`, and `myBill`
+If the prompt only asks for grep checks or a generic "page loads", that is too weak for a structural `CartView` rewrite.
+
+### Summary
+- Total findings: 8
+- Severity split: P1: 4, P2: 4
+- Most important prompt changes:
+  - define exact raw status-to-group mapping for Fix 1
+  - define whether Fix 3 is `CartView.jsx` only or also requires `x.jsx`
+  - scope-lock Fix 5 so split-type cleanup does not spill into unintended files
+  - replace "money only in header" with a precise surface-by-surface rule
+
+### Practical Recommendation
+Before implementation, the prompt should be revised to add:
+- a status mapping table
+- a file-scope section (`CartView.jsx` only vs `CartView.jsx` + `x.jsx`)
+- an explicit keep/remove matrix for header, table-total, status-group subtotal, new-order subtotal, and footer money
+- transition rules for auto-collapse
+- a verification checklist that includes parent-contract checks, not only UI screenshots or greps

**Findings**

- [P1] Fix 1 is under-specified. The prompt says “collapse 5 status buckets to 2 groups,” but the current component still groups by raw `order.status` in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:402) and still initializes five expand buckets in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:93). If the prompt does not explicitly map raw statuses like `served/completed` vs `ready/in_progress/accepted/new`, the implementation can collapse the wrong buckets.

- [P1] Fix 3 is incomplete unless the prompt widens scope beyond `CartView.jsx`. The save flow lives in [x.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:3297), and today it only exposes boolean `ratingSavingByItemId[itemId]`. There is no defined “A2” state contract in the parent. A prompt that asks for “submit feedback state A2” without defining where that state comes from is likely to produce invalid snippets or missing variables.

- [P1] Fix 5 is a scope/safety risk. The split UI is already gone from `CartView.jsx`, but dead prop plumbing still exists in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:32) and is still passed from [x.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/x.jsx:4771). “Remove split-type” is ambiguous unless the prompt explicitly says whether cleanup is `CartView.jsx` only or also includes `x.jsx`. Otherwise the implementer may touch files the prompt did not intend.

- [P1] Fix 2 is ambiguous. “Money only in header” is not precise enough because money currently appears in multiple places: header sum in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:417), table total card in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:842), status-group subtotals, and new-order subtotal. The prompt needs a keep/remove matrix for each money surface.

- [P2] Fix 4 needs transition semantics. The current auto-collapse effect only reacts to the `cart.length > 0` transition in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:96). The prompt should state whether collapse happens only on `0 -> >0`, on every cart mutation, and whether sections should reopen when the cart becomes empty again.

- [P2] Fix 6 is ambiguous across render paths. Quantity is not rendered in one place only; grouped status rows, cart rows, and table-order rows use different rules. “Fix qty display” needs to name every affected surface, or the implementer will likely patch one path and miss the others.

- [P2] Fix 7 is too subjective as written. The header currently includes optional call-waiter action, guest-name edit mode, count/sum line, and an `isSubmitting`-guarded close action in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:673). “Compact header” should define behavior for long table names, long guest names, no-bell layout, edit mode, and disabled-close state on mobile.

- [P2] Post-fix checks are too weak unless they verify both UI and contract cleanup. The prompt should require checks for empty vs non-empty cart, served-only state, rating save/fail/retry flow, narrow mobile header layout, and parent/child prop alignment between `x.jsx` and `CartView.jsx`. It should also explicitly check for leftover dead state like `showRewardEmailForm` in [CartView.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:114).

No P0 issue is evident from the available material, but the biggest prompt-design problem is scope ambiguity: several fixes read as `CartView.jsx`-only, while at least one of them clearly depends on `x.jsx`.
